<script id="chooseSizeTmpl" type="text/x-jsrender" data-jsv-tmpl="chooseSize">
    <h1 class="quick-order-popup-title">Выберите размер</h1>
    <div class="pp-sizes j-quick-order-sizes">
        {{for sizes}}
        {{if #data.s}}

                    userQuery = "\u0442\u0435\u0445\u043D\u0438\u043A\u0430 polaris",

                params.push(wb.stat.wrapParam("Q", query));
                params.push(wb.stat.wrapParam("UQ", userQuery));
                params.push(wb.stat.wrapParam("SRC", resultsCount || 0));

        (function ($) {
            var $container = $(".j-recent-goods-container");
            var action = loadVisitedGoods;
            
            onScroll($container, '.visited', action);

            function loadVisitedGoods(container) {
                //console.log('loadVisitedGoods');
                $.post("/visitedgoods", { count: container.attr("data-count") }, function (html) {
                    container.html(html);
                    wb.carousel.renderProductPrices(container, true);
                }, "html");
            }

            function onScroll(container, eventNameSpace, action) {
                var eventName = 'scroll' + eventNameSpace;
                $(window).on(eventName, function () {
                    if (!wb.utils.isElementInViewport(container, true))
                        return;

                    $(window).off(eventNameSpace);
                    action(container);
                }).trigger(eventName);
            }
        })(jQuery);
